### Historical American Civil War - USA vs CSA ###

	## Setup ##

		#Description: The Slavery Debate - Set Up - gain slave pops and consciousness
		country_event = {
			id = 16001
			title = "EVTNAME16001"
			desc = "EVTDESC16001"
			news = yes
			news_title = "EVTNAME16001_NEWS_TITLE"
			news_desc_long = "EVTDESC16001_NEWS_LONG"
			news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC16001_NEWS_MEDIUM"
			news_desc_short = "EVTDESC16001_NEWS_SHORT"
			picture = "Slaves"

			trigger = {
				tag = USA
				OR = {
					slavery = yes_slavery
					slavery = freedom_of_womb
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.01
					upper_house = {
						ideology = liberal
						value = 0.35
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
			}

			fire_only_once = yes

			immediate = {
				set_country_flag = the_slavery_debate
			}

			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA16001"

				any_owned = {
					limit = { has_pop_type = slaves trade_goods = cotton }
					slaves = { reduce_pop = 1.2 }
				}
				add_country_modifier = { name = the_slavery_debate_modifier duration = 10950 }
			}
		}

		#Description: John Brown's Raid - Dixie pops gain consciousness and militancy
		country_event = {
			id = 16010
			title = "EVTNAME16010"
			desc = "EVTDESC16010"
			news = yes
			news_desc_long = "EVTDESC16010_NEWS_LONG"
			news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC16010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
			news_desc_short = "EVTDESC16010_NEWS_SHORT"
			picture = "john_brown_raid"

			fire_only_once = yes

			trigger = {
				tag = USA
				slavery = yes_slavery
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = john_browns_raid
					has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
				}
				any_state = {
					is_slave = no
					average_consciousness = 6
				}
				upper_house = {
					ideology = liberal
					value = 0.1
				}
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 10
				modifier = {
					factor = 20
					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
			}

			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA16010"

				set_country_flag = john_browns_raid
				any_pop = {
					limit = { has_pop_culture = dixie }
					militancy = 1
					consciousness = 2
					ideology = {
						value = reactionary
						factor = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
		}

	## Flavor ##

		#Description: Dred Scott v. Sandford - Find for Scott or against him, angering either the north or the south
		country_event = {
			id = 16020
			title = "EVTNAME16020"
			desc = "EVTDESC16020"
			news = yes
			news_desc_long = "EVTDESC16020_NEWS_LONG"
			news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC16020_NEWS_MEDIUM"
			news_desc_short = "EVTDESC16020_NEWS_SHORT"
			picture = "dred_scott_v_sandford"

			fire_only_once = yes

			trigger = {
				tag = USA
				slavery = yes_slavery
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = dred_scott_decision
					has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
				}
				any_state = {
					is_slave = yes
					average_consciousness = 5
				}
				upper_house = {
					ideology = liberal
					value = 0.1
				}
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 10
				modifier = {
					factor = 20
					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
			}

			immediate = {
				set_country_flag = dred_scott_decision
			}

			# Find against Scott - he remains a slave
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA16020"

				any_pop = {
					limit = { has_pop_culture = yankee }
					militancy = 1
					consciousness = 2
					ideology = {
						value = liberal
						factor = 0.05
					}
				}
			}

			# Find for Scott - he is freed
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTB16020"

				any_pop = {
					limit = { has_pop_culture = dixie }
					militancy = 1
					consciousness = 2
					ideology = {
						value = reactionary
						factor = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
		}

		#Description: A Southern Belle
		country_event = {
			id = 16030
			title = "EVTNAME16030"
			desc = "EVTDESC16030"
			picture = "southern_belle"

			trigger = {
				tag = USA
				OR = {
					slavery = yes_slavery
					slavery = freedom_of_womb
				}
				any_state = {
					is_slave = yes
					is_colonial = no
					NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = southern_pride } }
					any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 20 #600
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 6
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					NOT = { average_consciousness = 5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 20
					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
			}

			# Slave state rich pops get conservative
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA16030"

				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_slave = yes
						is_colonial = no
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = southern_pride } }
						any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
					}
					aristocrats = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
					capitalists = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
					any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = southern_pride duration = 365 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 99
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_slave = yes
							is_colonial = no
							NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = southern_pride } }
							any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
						}
						aristocrats = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
						capitalists = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
						any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = southern_pride duration = 365 } }
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 75
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_slave = yes
							is_colonial = no
							NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = southern_pride } }
							any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
						}
						aristocrats = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
						capitalists = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
						any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = southern_pride duration = 365 } }
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 60
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_slave = yes
							is_colonial = no
							NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = southern_pride } }
							any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
						}
						aristocrats = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
						capitalists = { ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.05 } }
						any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = southern_pride duration = 365 } }
					}
				}
			}

		#Description: Southern Manorialism
		country_event = {
			id = 16040
			title = "EVTNAME16040"
			desc = "EVTDESC16040"

			trigger = {
				tag = USA
				OR = {
					slavery = yes_slavery
					slavery = freedom_of_womb

					NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = southern_manorialism } }
					any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 30 #600
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 6
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					NOT = { average_consciousness = 5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 20
					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
			}

		#Description: I Wish I Was in Dixie
		country_event = {
			id = 16050
			title = "EVTNAME16050"
			desc = "EVTDESC16050"
			picture = "dixie"

			trigger = {
				tag = USA
				OR = {
					slavery = yes_slavery
					slavery = freedom_of_womb
				}
				any_state = {
					is_slave = yes
					is_colonial = no
					NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = wish_I_was_dixie } }
					any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 40
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 6
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					NOT = { average_consciousness = 5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 20
					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
			}

			# Slave state free pops get conservative and consciousness
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA16050"

				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_slave = yes
						is_colonial = no
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = wish_I_was_dixie } }
						any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
					}
					any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = wish_I_was_dixie duration = 365 } }
					any_pop = {
						limit = { NOT = { type = slaves } }
						dominant_issue = { value = yes_slavery factor = 0.1 }
						ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.2 }
						consciousness = 2
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 99
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_slave = yes
							is_colonial = no
							NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = wish_I_was_dixie } }
							any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
						}
						any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = wish_I_was_dixie duration = 365 } }
						any_pop = {
							limit = { NOT = { type = slaves } }
							dominant_issue = { value = yes_slavery factor = 0.1 }
							ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.2 }
							consciousness = 2
						}
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 75
					random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_slave = yes
						is_colonial = no
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = wish_I_was_dixie } }
						any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
					}
					any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = wish_I_was_dixie duration = 365 } }
					any_pop = {
						limit = { NOT = { type = slaves } }
						dominant_issue = { value = yes_slavery factor = 0.1 }
						ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.2 }
						consciousness = 2
						}
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 60
					random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_slave = yes
						is_colonial = no
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = wish_I_was_dixie } }
						any_owned_province = { any_pop = { has_pop_culture = dixie } }
					}
					any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = wish_I_was_dixie duration = 365 } }

			desc = "EVTDESC16090"
			picture = "knights_golden_circle"


			trigger = {
				tag = USA
				OR = {
					slavery = yes_slavery
					slavery = freedom_of_womb
				}
				any_state = {
					is_colonial = no
					NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = knights_of_the_golden_circle } }
					any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { state_scope = { is_slave = yes } } }
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 20
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 6
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					NOT = { average_consciousness = 5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 20
					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
			}

			# Leave them be - free pops favor slavery and become reactionary
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA16090"

				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_colonial = no
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = knights_of_the_golden_circle } }
						any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { state_scope = { is_slave = yes } } }
					}
					any_owned = { add_province_modifier = { name = knights_of_the_golden_circle duration = 365 } }
					any_pop = {
						limit = { NOT = { type = slaves } }
						dominant_issue = { value = yes_slavery factor = 0.1 }
						ideology = { value = reactionary factor = 0.2 }
					}
				}
				random = {

			# Slave state poor pops gain consciousness, become liberal and favor freedom of womb and no slavery
			option = {

		#Description: Fugitive Slave
		country_event = {
			id = 16130
			title = "EVTNAME16130"
			desc = "EVTDESC16130"
			picture = "fugitive_slave"

				tag = USA
				OR = {
					slavery = yes_slavery
					slavery = freedom_of_womb
				}
				any_state = {
					is_colonial = no
					is_slave = no
					NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = fugitive_slave } }
					any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { state_scope = { is_slave = yes } } }
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = fugitive_slave_act_enacted }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = fugitive_slave }
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 20 #600

					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 5

					factor = 0.9
					average_consciousness = 6
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5

					factor = 20

					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}

					factor = 5

		country_event = {

				set_global_flag = csa_released

					NOT = { year = 1845 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					year = 1845
					NOT = { year = 1855 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					year = 1855
					NOT = { year = 1860 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					year = 1861
				}
			}

			#Play as USA
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA16000"

				any_pop = {
					limit = { has_pop_culture = dixie }

					consciousness = 2
					ideology = { value = reactionary factor = 0.05 }
				}
				remove_country_modifier = the_slavery_debate_modifier
				add_country_modifier = { name = no_more_war duration = 150 }
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						is_core = CSA
						NOT = {
							region = TEX_132 # Texas
							region = USA_148 # Missouri
							region = USA_185 # Kentucky
							region = USA_219 # Maryland
						}
					}
					secede_province = CSA
				}

				USA_185 = { add_core = UKY }
				any_owned = {
					limit = { region = USA_185 } # Kentucky
					secede_province = UKY
				}
				UKY = { add_country_modifier = { name = neutrality duration = -1 } }

				relation = { who = CSA value = 200 }
				diplomatic_influence = { who = CSA value = 400 }
				military_access = CSA
				create_alliance = CSA

				badboy = -1
				CSA = {
					ruling_party_ideology = conservative
					political_reform = mandatory_service
					political_reform = culture_voting_only
					capital = 60
					leadership = 80
					treasury = 40000
					small_arms = 300
					cotton = 100
					ammunition = 200
					canned_food = 200
					artillery = 100
					wine = 200
					liquor = 200
					any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_culture = dixie } militancy = -9 }
					random_pop = {
						limit = {
							pop_type = farmers
							has_pop_culture = dixie
						}
						pop_type = soldiers
					}
					add_country_modifier = { name = no_more_war duration = 150 }
				}
				country_event = { id = 16000 days = 150 } # Declaration of War
				CSA = { country_event = { id = 95264 days = 10 } } # Texas governor refuses secession
				CSA = { country_event = { id = 95263 days = 30 } } # Kentucky declared neutrality

				ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
			}

## Mexico in ACW ##

	#Description: If Mexico is not given autonomy, they will revolt alongside the CSA/FSA

				}
			}

			NOT = { exists = MEX }
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 5
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		# Keep them in the union - war in 120 days, cores if you win

			name = "EVTOPTA993888"

			set_country_flag = mexico_independence
			any_owned = { # Remove cores so USA can't just cheesily peace out nations and gobble them up later individually
				limit = { is_core = MEX }
				remove_core = USA
			}
			release_vassal = MEX
			diplomatic_influence = { who = MEX value = 200 }
			MEX = {
				leadership = 100
				small_arms = 750
				canned_food = 1500
				artillery = 750
				luxury_clothes = 250
				wine = 500
				liquor = 500
				add_country_modifier = { name = neutrality duration = 120 }
			}
			country_event = { id = 993889 days = 120 }

			ai_chance = { factor = 75 }
		}

		# Relase as vassal - no war, no cores
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTB993888"

			release_vassal = MEX

				leadership = 100

				}

					limit = {
						war_with = THIS

							tag = CSA
							tag = FSA
						}
						relation = { who = MEX value = 0 }
					}
					create_alliance = MEX
				}

			## Declare war ##
				random_owned = {
					limit = { USA = { any_owned_province = { is_core = MEX } } }
					USA = {
						war = {
							target = MEX
							attacker_goal = { casus_belli = civil_war }
							defender_goal = { casus_belli = status_quo }
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = { NOT = { USA = { any_owned_province = { is_core = MEX } } } }
					USA = {
						war = {
							target = MEX
							attacker_goal = { casus_belli = civil_war }
							defender_goal = { casus_belli = acquire_all_cores }
						}
					}
				}
		}
	}

		title = "EVTNAME993895"
		desc = "EVTDESC993895"
		picture = "mexico_city_occupation"

		trigger = {
			tag = USA
			has_country_flag = mexico_independence
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
				has_global_flag = alt_american_civil_war_has_happened
			}
			war = no
			NOT = { exists = MEX }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = mexico_integration_succeeded
				has_country_flag = mexico_integration_failed
			}
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 14
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		immediate = {
			set_country_flag = mexico_integration_succeeded
			set_global_flag = rio_grande_is_a_state
			set_global_flag = sonora_is_a_state
		}

		# Integrate Mexico as is - no assimilation of Mexican pops, but you will be able to accept them later
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA993895"

			prestige = 30
			badboy = 8
			all_core = { remove_core = MEX }
			any_owned = {
				limit = { is_core = MEX }
				add_core = USA
			}

			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = mexican }
				dominant_issue = { value = full_citizenship factor = 0.5 }
				dominant_issue = { value = no_slavery factor = 0.6 }
				consciousness = 5
			}

			ai_chance = {
				factor = 50
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { badboy = 0.48 }
				}
			}
		}

		# Anglify the north - remove MEX cores in the north to allow for assimilation, but you will be unable to accept Mexican culture later
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTB993895"

			prestige = 30
			badboy = 12
			MEX_2150 = { add_core = USA } # Rio Grande
			MEX_2149 = { add_core = USA } # Cohauila
			MEX_2142 = { add_core = USA } # Chihuahua
			MEX_2151 = { add_core = USA } # Durango
			MEX_2139 = { add_core = USA } # Baja California
			MEX_2138 = { add_core = USA } # Sonora
			MEX_2156 = { add_core = USA } # Sinaloa
			set_global_flag = usa_anglify_north_mexico
			all_core = { remove_core = MEX }
			any_owned = {
				limit = { is_core = MEX }
				add_core = USA
			}

			RGR = { primary_culture = yankee }

			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = mexican }
				dominant_issue = { value = full_citizenship factor = 0.6 }
				dominant_issue = { value = no_slavery factor = 0.75 }
				militancy = 2
				consciousness = 6
			}

			ai_chance = {
				factor = 50
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					badboy = 0.48
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Description: Integration of Mexican pops if North Mexico was not anglified
	country_event = {
		id = 993893
		title = "EVTNAME993893"
		desc = "EVTDESC993893"
		picture = "Cubanrebels"

		trigger = {
			tag = USA
			is_core = 2172 # Mexico City
			owns = 2172
			war = no
			is_disarmed = no
			has_recently_lost_war = no
			prestige = 500
			mass_politics = 1
			NOT = { has_global_flag = usa_anglify_north_mexico }
			has_country_flag = democracy_gov
			citizens_rights = all_voting_pops
			NOT = {
				average_militancy = 6
				num_of_revolts = 1
				national_provinces_occupied = 0.1
			}
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 60
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		# Accept Mexicans
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA993893"

			add_accepted_culture = mexican
			add_country_modifier = { name = usa_mexican_integration duration = 7300 } # 20 years
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_culture_group = american_cultures }
				scaled_militancy = { ideology = conservative factor = 3 }
				scaled_militancy = { ideology = reactionary factor = 5 }
				scaled_militancy = { issue = residency factor = 3 }
				scaled_militancy = { issue = limited_citizenship factor = 5 }
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = mexican }
				militancy = -3
				consciousness = -4
			}

			ai_chance = {
				factor = 99
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					ruling_party_ideology = fascist
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
				}
			}
		}

		# Don't accept Mexicans
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTB993893"

			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_culture_group = american_cultures }
				scaled_militancy = { ideology = conservative factor = -3 }
				scaled_militancy = { ideology = reactionary factor = -5 }
				scaled_militancy = { issue = residency factor = -3 }
				scaled_militancy = { issue = limited_citizenship factor = -5 }
			}
			any_pop = {
				scaled_consciousness = { issue = all_voting_pops factor = 4 }
				dominant_issue = { value = culture_voting_only factor = 0.2 }
				ideology = { value = conservative factor = 0.2 }
				ideology = { value = reactionary factor = 0.2 }
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = mexican }
				militancy = 6
				consciousness = 8
			}

			ai_chance = {
				factor = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = fascist }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = reactionary }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Description: Second Constitutional Convention - FSA cores start, upper house is not population equal weight
	country_event = {
		id = 16500
		title = "EVTNAME16500"
		desc = "EVTDESC16500"
		news = yes
		news_desc_long = "EVTDESC16500_NEWS_LONG"
		news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC16500_NEWS_MEDIUM"
		news_desc_short = "EVTDESC16500_NEWS_SHORT"
		picture = "senate_debate"

		trigger = {
			tag = USA
			OR = {
				year = 1865
				has_global_flag = fil_annexed_by_usa
			}
			NOT = { exists = CSA }
			OR = {
				slavery = yes_slavery
				slavery = freedom_of_womb
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = john_browns_raid
				has_global_flag = fil_annexed_by_usa
			}
			has_country_flag = dred_scott_decision
			NOT = {
				exists = CSA
				upper_house_composition = population_equal_weight
				has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
				has_country_flag = second_constitutional_convention
			}
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 36
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				war_exhaustion = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_greater_power = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				year = 1868
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				year = 1870
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				year = 1875
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_global_flag = fil_annexed_by_usa
			}
		}

		immediate = {
			set_variable = {
				which = FSA_states
				value = 1
			}
		}

		# Convention will move forward
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA16500"

			set_country_flag = second_constitutional_convention
			political_reform = population_equal_weight
			random_owned = { # FSA cores
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = USA_223 # Pennsylvania
						region = USA_232 # New York
						region = USA_243 # Massachusets
					}
				}
				state_scope = { any_owned = { add_core = FSA } }
			}

			any_state = { # Slave state pops favor state equal weight and become reactionary
				limit = {
					is_slave = yes
					is_colonial = no
				}
				any_pop = {
					dominant_issue = {
						value = state_equal_weight
						factor = 0.20
					}
					ideology = {
						value = reactionary
						factor = 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			any_state = { # Free state pops become liberal
				limit = {
					is_slave = no
					is_colonial = no
				}
				any_pop = {
					ideology = {
						value = liberal
						factor = 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				scaled_consciousness = {
					ideology = conservative
					factor = 6
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					ideology = reactionary
					factor = 6
				}
			}
		}

		# Constitution shall not be amended
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTB16500"

			set_country_flag = second_constitutional_convention
			random_owned = { # FSA cores
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = USA_223 # Pennsylvania
						region = USA_232 # New York
						region = USA_243 # Massachusets
					}
				}
				state_scope = { any_owned = { add_core = FSA } }
			}

			# Free state pops favor abolitionism
			any_state = {
				limit = {
					country = { slavery = freedom_of_womb }
					is_slave = no
					is_colonial = no
				}
				any_pop = {
					dominant_issue = {
						value = no_slavery
						factor = 0.20
					}
					ideology = {
						value = liberal
						factor = 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			any_state = {
				limit = {
					country = { slavery = yes_slavery }
					is_slave = no
					is_colonial = no
				}
				any_pop = {
					dominant_issue = {
						value = freedom_of_womb
						factor = 0.20
					}
					ideology = {
						value = liberal
						factor = 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			any_state = { # Slave state pops become conservative
				limit = {
					is_slave = yes
					is_colonial = no
				}
				any_pop = {
					ideology = {
						value = conservative
						factor = 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				scaled_consciousness = {
					ideology = liberal
					factor = 6
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					ideology = anarcho_liberal
					factor = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
			any_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							any_owned_province = { is_core = USA }
							NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_core = CSA } }
						}
						AND = {
							any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = FSA } }
							any_owned_province = {
								is_core = USA
								culture = yankee
							}
						}
					}
				}
				any_owned = { add_core = FSA }
			}
			war = {
				target = FSA
				attacker_goal = { casus_belli = civil_war }
				defender_goal = { casus_belli = status_quo }
			}

			ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		}
	}

	#Description: The Union Sundered - If the USA loses against the FSA, they will become the CSA

				owner = { capital = 60 } # Richmond
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = dixie }
				dominant_issue = {
					factor = 0.10
					value = jingoism
				}
				ideology = {
					value = reactionary
					factor = 0.10
				}
			}
			change_tag = CSA
			remove_accepted_culture = yankee
			set_country_flag = the_slavery_debate
			any_state = {
				limit = {
					is_slave = no
					NOT = {
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								culture = dixie
								culture = texan
								is_core = TEX
							}
						}
					}
				}
				any_owned = { remove_core = CSA }
			}
			any_country = {
				any_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_owned_province = {
								OR = {
									culture = dixie
									culture = texan
									is_core = TEX
								}
							}
						}
					}
					any_owned = { remove_core = CSA }
				}
			}
		}

### Second American Civil War - Disunited States ###

	#Description: The Disunited States - If the USA is not a democracy
	country_event = {

		id = 95260
		title = "EVTNAME95260"
		desc = "EVTDESC95260"
		news = yes
		news_desc_long = "EVTDESC95260_NEWS_LONG"
		news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC95260_NEWS_MEDIUM"
		news_desc_short = "EVTDESC95260_NEWS_SHORT"
		picture = "Demonstration"

		major = yes
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
			war = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = democracy_gov }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = disunited_states }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = begin_disunited_states }
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
				has_global_flag = alt_american_civil_war_has_happened
			}
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 24
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				vote_franschise = none_voting
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { vote_franschise = none_voting }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				national_provinces_occupied = .01
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				num_of_revolts = 1
			}
		}

		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA95260"

			set_global_flag = disunited_states
			set_global_flag = second_american_civil_war
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = begin_disunited_states
				duration = 3650
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					location = { is_core = USA }
					OR = {
						is_primary_culture = yes
						is_accepted_culture = yes
					}
					OR = {
						pop_majority_ideology = liberal
						liberal = 30
						anarcho_liberal = 20
					}
				}
				ideology = { factor = 0.3 value = liberal }
				consciousness = 5
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_province = { is_core = USA }
					NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
					liberal = 30
				}
				any_owned = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = sons_of_liberty
						duration = 365
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Description: Sons of Liberty
	province_event = {

		id = 95261
		title = "EVTNAME95261"
		desc = "EVTDESC95261"

		trigger = {
			owner = {
				tag = USA
				has_global_flag = disunited_states
				has_country_modifier = begin_disunited_states
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = sons_of_liberty }
			OR = {
				average_consciousness = 7
				average_militancy = 4
				controlled_by_rebels = yes
			}
			OR = {
				controlled_by_rebels = yes
				liberal = 30
				anarcho_liberal = 20
				AND = {
					liberal = 20
					OR = {
						any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = sons_of_liberty }
						any_neighbor_province = {
							NOT = { owned_by = USA }
							NOT = { owned_by = ENG }
							NOT = { owned_by = CAN }
							NOT = { owned_by = MEX }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			is_core = USA
			is_colonial = no
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = sons_of_liberty }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = sons_of_liberty } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { liberal = 40 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { state_scope = { average_militancy = 2 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				state_scope = { average_militancy = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				state_scope = { average_militancy = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				controlled_by_rebels = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				state_scope = { any_owned_province = { country_units_in_province = USA } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				any_neighbor_province = {
					NOT = { owned_by = USA }
					NOT = { owned_by = ENG }
					NOT = { owned_by = CAN }
					NOT = { owned_by = MEX }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = { has_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov }
			}
		}

						ideology = liberal

					}
				}
			}
		}

		#Description: Congress of $STATENAME$ - state joins CSA
		province_event = {
			id = 95268
			title = "EVTNAME95266"
			desc = "EVTDESC95268"

			trigger = {
				owned_by = USA
				is_core = CSA
				is_colonial = no
				state_scope = { NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } } }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						controlled_by = REB
						province_control_days = 120
						NOT = { country_units_in_province = USA }
					}
					AND = {
						has_province_modifier = sons_of_liberty
						OR = {
							controlled_by = REB
							average_militancy = 8
						}
						state_scope = {
							OR = {
								liberal = 30
								anarcho_liberal = 20
							}
							average_militancy = 4
						}
					}
				}
				CSA = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						num_of_revolts = 1
						is_disarmed = yes
						truce_with = USA
					}
					OR = {
						war = no
						NOT = { national_provinces_occupied = .25 }
					}
				}
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 40
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.8
					state_scope = { average_militancy = 5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.8
					state_scope = { average_militancy = 6 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.8
					state_scope = { average_militancy = 7 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.8
					state_scope = { average_militancy = 8 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					OR = {
						FSA = { exists = yes }
						UNB = { exists = yes }
						UIL = { exists = yes }
						NEN = { exists = yes }
						DAK = { exists = yes }
						UOR = { exists = yes }
						CAL = { exists = yes }
						TEX = { exists = yes }
						UNM = { exists = yes }
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					owner = { has_country_flag = democracy_gov }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					owner = { has_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov }
				}
			}

			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA95266"

				state_scope = {
					any_owned = {
						limit = { is_core = CSA }
						any_pop = {

								factor = -8
							}
						}

					}

		#Description: The Halifax Convention - Maritime Union secedes - if Crusade for Canada
		country_event = {

							}

						truce_with = USA
					}

						war = no
						NOT = { national_provinces_occupied = .25 }
					}
				}
			}

						UOR = { exists = yes }

					has_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov
				}
			}

			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA95260"

				set_country_flag = CHP_created
				prestige = -50
				2181 = { add_core = CHP } # Tuxtla
				2182 = { add_core = CHP } # Soconusco
				any_state = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_province = {
							is_core = CHP
							OR = {
								AND = {
									controlled_by = REB
									province_control_days = 120
									NOT = { country_units_in_province = USA }
								}
								AND = {
									has_province_modifier = sons_of_liberty
									OR = {
										controlled_by = REB
										average_militancy = 8
									}
									state_scope = {
										OR = {
											liberal = 30
											anarcho_liberal = 20
										}
										average_militancy = 4
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					any_owned = {
						limit = { is_core = CHP }
						change_controller = THIS
						secede_province = CHP
					}
				}
				CHP = {
					set_country_flag = usstatehood_we_have_applied
					government = democracy
					ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					political_reform = universal_voting
					political_reform = population_equal_weight
					political_reform = yes_meeting
					political_reform = free_press
					political_reform = non_socialist
					political_reform = secret_ballots
					capital = 2181
					leadership = 40
					any_pop = {
						scaled_militancy = {
							ideology = liberal
							factor = -8
						}
					}
				}
				relation = { who = CHP value = -200 }
				diplomatic_influence = { who = CHP value = -200 }
				any_pop = {
					scaled_militancy = {
						ideology = liberal
						factor = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		#Description: Join the Canadian Confederation? - American minors can choose whether to ask to join Canada
		country_event = {

			id = 95315
			title = "EVTNAME95315"
			desc = "EVTDESC95315"
			picture = "administration"

			trigger = {
				OR = {
					tag = LSK # Alaska
					tag = NEN # New England
					tag = DAK # Dakota
					tag = UOR # Oregon
				}
				war = no
				is_greater_power = no
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = asked_to_join_canada
					in_sphere = USA
				}
				has_global_flag = second_american_civil_war
				neighbour = CAN
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = democracy_gov
					has_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov
				}
				OR = {
					in_sphere = CAN
					alliance_with = CAN
					relation = { who = CAN value = 50 }
					tag = LSK
					tag = NEN
				}
				CAN = {
					is_vassal = no
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = democracy_gov
						has_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov
					}
				}
			}

			mean_time_to_happen = {
				months = 40
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					ruling_party_ideology = liberal
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					OR = {
						alliance_with = CAN
						in_sphere = CAN
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					CAN = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					part_of_sphere = yes
					NOT = { in_sphere = CAN }
				}
			}

			# Ask to join
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA95315"

				set_country_flag = asked_to_join_canada
				prestige = -10
				CAN = { country_event = 95316 }

				ai_chance = {
					factor = 60
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						OR = {
							tag = LSK
							tag = NEN
						}
					}
				}
			}

			# Don't ask to join
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTB95315"

				set_country_flag = asked_to_join_canada
				prestige = 2

				ai_chance = {
					factor = 40
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						is_secondary_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		#Description: Triggered for Canada when American minors decide to ask to join.
		country_event = {

			id = 95316
			title = "EVTNAME95316"
			desc = "EVTDESC95316"
			major = yes

			is_triggered_only = yes

			# Accept
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTA95316"

				prestige = 20
				FROM = { all_core = { add_core = CAN } }
				inherit = FROM
				random_owned = {
					limit = { owner = { NOT = { accepted_culture = yankee } } }
					owner = { add_accepted_culture = yankee }
				}
				USA = {
					relation = { who = CAN value = -50 }
					diplomatic_influence = { who = CAN value = -50 }
					casus_belli = { target = CAN type = humiliate months = 60 }
				}

				ai_chance = {
					factor = 50
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						FROM = { NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { is_core = CAN } } } }
					}
				}
			}

			# Refuse
			option = {
				name = "EVTOPTB95316"

				relation = { who = FROM value = -25 }
				relation = { who = USA value = 25 }

				ai_chance = {
					factor = 50
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						FROM = { tag = NEN }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						FROM = { tag = UOR }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						FROM = { NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { is_core = CAN } } } }
					}
				}
			}
